<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:normal'><strong><i
style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:20.0pt;

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:normal'><strong><i
style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:20.0pt;

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoSubtitle><a name="_Toc352593007"><span class=MsoSubtleEmphasis><span
lang=EN-US style='font-style:normal'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></a></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc352593007'><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc352593007'><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc352593007'><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc352593007'><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc352593007'><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></p>

<div style='mso-element:para-border-div;border:none;border-bottom:solid #4F81BD 1.0pt;
mso-border-bottom-themecolor:accent1;padding:0cm 0cm 4.0pt 0cm'>

<p class=MsoTitle><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc352593007'><span lang=EN-US>Abstract</span></span></p>

</div>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The aim of this project is to create a smartphone
application that utilises the unique capabilities of smartphones in order to
aid the personal security for vulnerable individuals.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The application was designed to utilise a
smartphones built-in GPS and accelerometer to track the users location and
detect scenarios in which the user may be in a vulnerable situation. This
involves detection of scenarios such as a user physically falling, or veering
outside a particular boundary when such behavior is unexpected of them. When
possible (i.e. User device has Internet connectivity) a users location data is
uploaded to a backend server where other users of the application can query
their most recent location and the time at which they were present at that
location. The application also has the ability to send an emergency SMS in the case
of an emergency such as a fall being detected or a user travelling outside of a
pre-defined boundary (i.e. The boundary being a pre-defined distance from their
starting position).</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The application was designed, developed and
deployed on the Android platform using the Android Studio IDE.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The project also incorporates the use of
both PHP and MySQL to develop the supporting backend remote database server.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The project meets the primary aims of allowing
periodic check-ins from a users smartphone, remote monitoring of smartphone device
location, detection of lack of user movement (i.e. the implementation of fall
detection) and movement outside certain boundaries.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<div style='mso-element:para-border-div;border:none;border-bottom:solid #4F81BD 1.0pt;
mso-border-bottom-themecolor:accent1;padding:0cm 0cm 4.0pt 0cm'>

mso-border-bottom-themecolor:accent1;padding:0cm 0cm 4.0pt 0cm'>

<p class=MsoTitle><a name="_Toc352593009"></a><a name="_Toc351129866"><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc352593009'><span lang=EN-US>1. </span></span></a><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc352593009'><span lang=EN-US>Introduction</span></span></p>

</div>

<h1><a name="_Toc352593010"><span lang=EN-US>1.1<span style='mso-tab-count:
1'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Background</span></a></h1>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>Personal security has always been a very
important issue as no matter how adequate the personal security measures in
place are it is always something that can be enhanced. Security is especially an
issue for more vulnerable people such as younger children and the elderly. This
is because of hazards such as getting lost, going missing or suffering a fall.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>Over the last number of years there has
been a staggering amount of missing people reported in Ireland alone. For
example in 2013 there were approximately 7700 people reported missing and in
2014 there were approximately 9100 people reported missing. [4] </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>Injuries due to falls are commonplace
especially among the elderly in our population. It is estimated the 1/3 of the
population over 65 years old have a fall causing injury each year. [5] </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>According to statistics gathered by
IrishHealth there are approximately 7000 people over 65 are admitted to
hospital with injuries relating to a fall each year. [6]<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp; </span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>Due to the advancements in smartphone
capabilities gives rise to the possibility of enhancing personal security.
These advancements allow things such as location tracking, fall detection, SMS
transmission without user interaction &amp; boundary detection.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>According to figures accumulated in 2015 2.37m
people in Ireland own a smartphone with 55% of that 70% owning an android
smartphone. [7][8]</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The issues with personal security and the
advancement in capabilities of smartphones are what inspired the idea behind
TrackMe.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>TrackMe is an application that provides the
functionality of user location tracking, boundary tracking &amp; fall
detection. Location information is uploaded to the backend server where it can
be analysed and other TrackMe users can track a users latest location via their
username. If a fall is detected or if a user passes outside a specified
boundary an SMS will be sent to a user defined emergency contact.</span></p>

<h1><a name="_Toc352593011"><span lang=EN-US>1.2<span style='mso-tab-count:
1'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Project Objectives</span></a></h1>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>This project involved the creation of a
fully functional smartphone application and the application was designed to
provide the end user with the following core features:</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l15 level1 lfo1'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Application tracks user
location at a user-specified time interval.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l15 level1 lfo1'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>User can query another users
latest location update from server.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l15 level1 lfo1'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>User can enable fall detection
algorithm.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l15 level1 lfo1'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>User can enable boundary detection
from tracking start point.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>These core features required the following
to also be implemented in the project:</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l22 level1 lfo2'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Allowing the application to upload
location data to backend server when possible (i.e. Internet connection is available
on user device).</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l22 level1 lfo2'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Allowing the application
permission to access devices system services and hardware such as Internet, accelerometer
&amp; GPS location hardware.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The goal is to implement these features
with a user-friendly interface.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The main purpose of the application is to
enhance the personal security of the user by providing means by which to alert
others of possible danger to them &amp; also be able to track the users latest
location, using their username, if they are deemed to be in any form of unexpected
situation or a fall has been detected.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h1><a name="_Toc352593012"><span lang=EN-US>1.3<span style='mso-tab-count:
1'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Context</span></a></h1>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>Additional objectives and motivations that
I had for undertaking this project are as follows:</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc352593013"><span lang=EN-US>1.3.1<span style='mso-tab-count:
1'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Mobile Application Development</span></a></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>I have always been interested in developing
smartphones applications but prior to undertaking this project I was always
under too many time constraints to afford me the opportunity to attempt some mobile
app development. I saw this project as a great opportunity to develop an
application of my own and gain some knowledge about mobile application
development.</span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc352593014"><span lang=EN-US>1.3.2<span style='mso-tab-count:
1'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Learn Server-Side Scripting Language</span></a></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>Throughout the completion of my degree I
was never afforded the opportunity to undertake any great amount of development
using a server side scripting language such as PHP or Ruby. I used this project
as an opportunity to develop my knowledge of PHP by using it to complete
server-side scripting.</span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc352593015"><span lang=EN-US>1.3.3<span style='mso-tab-count:
1'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Database Administration</span></a><span lang=EN-US> </span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>During the completion of my degree I have
already gained some experience in the setup and administration of databases,
such as MySQL and Microsoft SQL Server, but I wanted to improve on my current
level of proficiency by setting up a more complex backend server than I have
used in previous projects.</span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc352593016"><span lang=EN-US>1.3.4<span style='mso-tab-count:
1'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Application Use</span></a></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>Having previously been in situations where
I would have found an application such as TrackMe useful I believed that this
project was interesting to see how I would be able to aid people in scenarios
where their personal security was compromised.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<div style='mso-element:para-border-div;border:none;border-bottom:solid #4F81BD 1.0pt;
mso-border-bottom-themecolor:accent1;padding:0cm 0cm 4.0pt 0cm'>

<p class=MsoTitle><a name="_Toc352593017"></a><a name="_Toc351129867"><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc352593017'><span lang=EN-US>2. </span></span></a><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc352593017'><span lang=EN-US>Technology Overview &amp;
Selection</span></span></p>

</div>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>This chapter is a state of the art review
of the technologies that are relevant to this project. It includes a brief
overview of current technologies available that I have investigated during the
completion of this project. This chapter also includes a review of products
&amp; services available that offer similar features to this project.</span></p>

<h1><a name="_Toc352593018"><span lang=EN-US>2.1<span style='mso-tab-count:
1'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Technology Overview</span></a></h1>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc352593019"><span lang=EN-US>2.1.1<span style='mso-tab-count:
1'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Mobile Application Platform</span></a></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>In this section I will discuss the possible
different platform that I could have used to develop TrackMe and the advantages
and disadvantages of these platforms.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The platforms that I investigated as part
of the project were Android and iOS as the project specification gave the
freedom to utilize a platform of my choice. I felt that these were the most
appropriate platforms given that theyÕre the two most popular platforms
worldwide. </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>An example of their popularity is that for
the year ending December 2016 there were approximately 1,270.000 Android
smartphones sold and in the same timeframe there were approximately 216,000 iOS
Devices sold. [9]</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc352593020"><span lang=EN-US>Android Platform</span></a><span
lang=EN-US><span style='mso-tab-count:1'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>Android is a mobile device operating system
built primarily for use with smartphones and tablets. Androids UI is based on
emulating real world direct manipulations such as tapping, swiping &amp;
dragging on-screen objects in order to manipulate them.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h4><a name="_Toc352593021"><span lang=EN-US>Advantages of Android Development</span></a></h4>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l2 level1 lfo6'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Significantly larger user base in
comparison to any other smartphone operating system meaning that applications
developed for Android devices have a much larger potential reach.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l2 level1 lfo6'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Online documentation for
Android development is largely accessible and very thorough.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l2 level1 lfo6'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Predominantly coded in Java
which is the programming language that I am most familiar with.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l2 level1 lfo6'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Deployment to Android
application store, i.e. Google Play Store, is a much simpler &amp; less costly
process than deployment of an iOS application to the App Store.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l2 level1 lfo6'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>The Android development
platform allows the use of third-party tools and libraries so allows a very
broad range of functionality within applications.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l2 level1 lfo6'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Broad range of possible
development environments can be used to develop applications such as Eclipse
&amp; Android Studio.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h4><a name="_Toc352593022"><span lang=EN-US>Disadvantages of Android
Development</span></a></h4>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l14 level1 lfo7'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Application development can be
more difficult due to the lenient implementation constraints applied to
development practices thus leading to the potential for an increased number of bugs.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l14 level1 lfo7'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>There is a large fragmentation
of operating system versions meaning that development of features need to be
carefully considered as they could potentially prevent a significant portion of
the potential market from being able application to run the application on
their device. </span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l14 level1 lfo7'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Large array of devices to consider
for UI compatibility.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc352593023"><span lang=EN-US>iOS Platform</span></a></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>iOS is a mobile device operating system
built exclusively for Apple devices such as the iPhone &amp; the iPad.
Similarly to Android the UI is based on the emulations of real world gestures.</span></p>

<h4><a name="_Toc352593024"><span lang=EN-US>Advantages of iOS Development</span></a></h4>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l21 level1 lfo8'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>iOS development features quite
rigourous development constraints which lead to an application which can often
be to a higher standard in comparison to other operating systemsÕ application.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l21 level1 lfo8'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Smaller array of possible
devices to develop for meaning that it is easier to develop application that is
compatible with the UI of all devices.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l21 level1 lfo8'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>More likely to be compatible
with most devices as there is less fragmentation of operating system releases.</span></p>

<h4><a name="_Toc352593025"><span lang=EN-US>Disadvantages of iOS Development</span></a></h4>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l20 level1 lfo9'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Much smaller potential user
base in comparison to the Android platform.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l20 level1 lfo9'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Development on the iOS platform
requires XCode IDE that is only available on Apple branded computers through
the iOS App Store.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l20 level1 lfo9'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>The process of deploying an
application to the App Store is costly, time consuming and has an expansive
level of auditing.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h4><a name="_Toc352593026"><span lang=EN-US>Platform Selection</span></a></h4>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>For the development of this application I
decided to use the Android platform as it allowed me to access the largest user
base and gave more freedom when developing as it allows for the use of many 3<sup>rd</sup>
party libraries during. </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc352593027"><span lang=EN-US>2.1.2<span style='mso-tab-count:
1'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Application Technologies</span></a></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>In this section I will discuss the possible
methods of implementing the key features of the application at a high level. I
will also give an insight into my rationale for my technology selection throughout
the course of TrackMeÕs development.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc352593028"><span lang=EN-US>Location Tracking</span></a></h3>

<h4><a name="_Toc352593029"><span lang=EN-US>Considerations</span></a></h4>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>Implementation could be achieved using GPS
location sensors on phone when location services are activated. </span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'>&#8232;</span><span
lang=EN-US>The smartphone devices could user itÕs network provider to detect a
users location when GPS is turned inactive. </span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'>&#8232; </span><span
lang=EN-US>A user could be tracked by either sending their location through a
network socket to another user or by uploading their location information to a
backend server where another user can query their location updates.</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'> </span><span
lang=EN-US>Throughout my research it became clear that a users address is only
available when they have an Internet connection on their device as there is no
alternative way to access a Geocoder. I did not consider this to be a major
problem as a user can still obtain their latitude and longitude values without
needing a connection.</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;
mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h4><a name="_Toc352593030"><span lang=EN-US>Selection</span></a></h4>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>For the development of this application I
decided to implement the following:</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='margin-left:39.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l18 level1 lfo13'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>A method that would receive the
most accurate location data at all times depending on the network and Internet
connectivity states of the device. (I.e. Use best available to device at the
time)</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo12'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Location data would be pushed
to the backend server, using an Internet connection. I considered the fact
needing an internet connection may be a problem but in recent times having
always on Internet connections on smartphone devices has become commonplace so
I decided that this would be the most secure and robust way to make user
location data available to the necessary individuals.</span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc352593031"><span lang=EN-US>Fall Detection</span></a></h3>

<h4><a name="_Toc352593032"><span lang=EN-US>Considerations</span></a></h4>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>Fall detection could be implemented in
several ways using a smartphone devices accelerometer. Fall detection can be
programmed to be either very sensitive or very ignorant to possible falls.
Generally speaking a fall is illustrated on a devicesÕ accelerometer by a
sudden spike in gravitational direction. Another consideration that needed to
be made was that the phone accelerometer would pick up natural gravitational
pull of approximately 9.8m/s at idle.</span></p>

<h4><a name="_Toc352593033"><span lang=EN-US>Selection</span></a></h4>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>For the development of a fall detection
algorithm I decided that the best approach would be to create an algorithm that
was quite sensitive as for the purpose of personal safety I felt that a false
positive was a better outcome than a false negative when detecting a fall.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc352593034"><span lang=EN-US>Messaging Service</span></a></h3>

<h4><a name="_Toc352593035"><span lang=EN-US>Considerations</span></a></h4>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>There is a range of possible social media
platforms that can be used for messaging such as Viber, Whatsapp and Facebook
Messenger applications as well as standard SMS services. For this application
the fundamental characteristic I wanted for my messaging platform was that a
message could be sent without any user input or interaction. I felt this was a fundamental
requirement as the messaging feature of the application would only be used in
case of emergency.</span></p>

<h4><a name="_Toc352593036"><span lang=EN-US>Selection</span></a></h4>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>I decided to use SMS as the applicationsÕ
messaging service as it was the only viable option that could send an emergency
message without the need for any user interaction. I felt that this was the
best option considering that this functionality would only be used in cases
where a possible danger or an emergency has been detected.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc352593037"><span lang=EN-US>2.1.3<span style='mso-tab-count:
1'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Web Hosting Service</span></a><span lang=EN-US> </span></h2>

<h3><a name="_Toc352593038"><span lang=EN-US>Considerations</span></a></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>For Implementation of a web server there
were many viable options such as Amazon Web Services, Google Web Server and NUI
GalwayÕs Danu6 Linux server.</span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc352593039"><span lang=EN-US>Selection</span></a></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>I decided to use NUI GalwayÕs DANU6 Linux
web server as it already had all the technologies I would possibly need to
complete my project.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>Danu6 is a Gentoo Linux cluster that runs:</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo12'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Apache 2.4 and MySQL 5.5</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo12'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>PHP 5.5 </span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo12'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Java 1.7</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo12'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Python 2.7 &amp; 3.3, </span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo12'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>PhpMyAdmin PHP 5.5</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc352593040"><span lang=EN-US>2.1.4<span style='mso-tab-count:
1'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Server Side Scripting</span></a></h2>

<h3><a name="_Toc352593041"><span lang=EN-US>Considerations</span></a></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>For this part of the project I considered
server-side scripting language such as Ruby and PHP.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp; </span>Both of these languages very easily are
able to accomplish what I needed from my server interaction.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc352593042"><span lang=EN-US>Selection</span></a></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>I decided to use PHP as it would easily
accomplish what I needed and it looked like Ruby had a much steeper learning
curve. PHP also had an abundance of online information and tutorials that would
be very useful if I was to run into problems.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc352593043"><span lang=EN-US>2.1.5 Database</span></a></h2>

<h3><a name="_Toc352593044"><span lang=EN-US>Considerations</span></a></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>For the implementation of a database to
store user profile and location details I considered several viable options
such as Microsoft SQL Server, MySQL and MongoDB. All of these above options can
be setup on NUI GalwayÕs Danu6 server and offer you a network accessible
database with full user authorisation and control.</span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc352593045"><span lang=EN-US>Selection</span></a></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>I decided to use a MySQL server as I had
previous experience in administering a MySQL database and it offered all the
functionality that I needed from a database.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span><span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></p>

<h1><a name="_Toc352593046"><span lang=EN-US>2.2<span style='mso-tab-count:
1'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Similar Applications</span></a></h1>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>During the development of any project it is
important to identify if similar products already exist or whether your project
offers something unique as then there is the potential to obtain a patent for
your idea.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>In my research of applications that provide
similar functionality to the proposed features of TrackMe I have found several
applications. These include BSafe, Emergensee. DigitalLife, Family Locator and
SafeTrek.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>All these applications are Android based
personal security applications. Some share common features with TrackMe but
ultimately they all have the same goal of augmenting the personal security of
individuals. </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The features of each of these applications
are outlined below. </span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:Times;
mso-bidi-font-family:Times'>&#8232;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:Times;mso-bidi-font-family:
Times'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc352593047"><span lang=EN-US>2.2.1<span style='mso-tab-count:
1'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>bSafe</span></a><span lang=EN-US> </span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>One of the applications I found with

<h2><a name="_Toc352593049"><span lang=EN-US>2.2.3 DigitalLife</span></a></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>Personal security application DigitalLife
is another app operating in the domain of personal security. [12]</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>It offers the following features:</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l25 level1 lfo20'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Send messages to frequent
contacts from within the application.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l25 level1 lfo20'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Share location information with
Monitoring Center Professionals in emergency situations.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l25 level1 lfo20'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Use a countdown timer in
uncomfortable situations that will send an alert to the monitoring center when
the time expires (e.g.: walking to the car alone late at night).</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoCaption align=center style='text-align:center'><a

<h2><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc352593050"><span lang=EN-US>2.2.4 Family Locator</span></a></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>Another personal security Android
application I discovered during my research was Family Locator. [14] </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>It offers the following features:</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l3 level1 lfo22'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Create your own groups, called
ÒCircles,Ó of loved ones, friends, teammates etc.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l3 level1 lfo22'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>View real-time location of
members on private map</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l3 level1 lfo22'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Receive real-time alerts when
ÒCircleÓ members leave or arrive a destination. </span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='margin-left:144.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;page-break-after:avoid'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape
 id="Picture_x0020_38" o:spid="_x0000_i1062" type="#_x0000_t75" alt="Description: Macintosh HD:Users:matthew:Downloads:unnamed.png"
 style='width:169pt;height:185pt;visibility:visible;mso-wrap-style:square'
 o:bordertopcolor="black" o:borderleftcolor="black" o:borderbottomcolor="black"
 o:borderrightcolor="black">
 <v:imagedata src="TrackMe_Project_Report_files/image011.png" o:title="unnamed.png"
  croptop="20970f" cropbottom="4201f"/>
 <w:bordertop type="single" width="6"/>
 <w:borderleft type="single" width="6"/>
 <w:borderbottom type="single" width="6"/>
 <w:borderright type="single" width="6"/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img width=171 height=187
src="TrackMe_Project_Report_files/image012.png"
alt="Description: Macintosh HD:Users:matthew:Downloads:unnamed.png" v:shapes="Picture_x0020_38"><![endif]></span></p>

<p class=MsoCaption style='margin-left:108.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt'><a
name="_Toc352537135"></a><a name="_Toc352536921"><span style='mso-bookmark:
_Toc352537135'><span lang=EN-US>Figure 2-2&#8209;4 Family Locator Application</span></span></a></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc352593051"><span lang=EN-US>2.2.5 SafeTrek</span></a></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>SafeTrek is a personal security application
that offers users the ability to make a passive connection to emergency
services if they feel they are in danger. This is achieved with minimal user
interaction and serves as the only functionality involved in the application.
[15]</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc352593052"><span lang=EN-US>2.2.6 Conclusion</span></a></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>It is clear from my research that there
isnÕt any patentable functionality present in the TrackMe application as any
key purpose of the application has already been implemented in other personal
security applications.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>Of the products that I have researched
during the development of TrackMe it seems that Emergensee, BSafe and Digital
Life all contain similar features to that of TrackMe.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span lang=EN-US>BSafe</span></i><span
lang=EN-US> offers location sharing and tracking similar to TrackMe. It also
offers guardian alert but rather than it being in the case of detection of a
possible emergency situation it offers this functionality through the means of
a button press. Emergensee offers similar features to TrackMe such as remote
location monitoring, pre-set safety contacts &amp; SMS distress messages.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>DigitalLife also shares some common ground
with TrackMe as it has the ability to send SMS distress messages and it
implements remote location monitoring. It also implements a countdown timer
before sending a distress signal in a similar way to TrackMe.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>FamilyLocator offers similar features to
that of TrackMe such as location tracking and remote monitoring of othersÕ
locations but seems to operate in a more specialised manner with the
introduction of groups.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>SafeTrek operates in the personal security
domain but there are no similar features present that are comparable to <i
style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>TrackMe</i>. </span></p>

<div style='mso-element:para-border-div;border:none;border-bottom:solid #4F81BD 1.0pt;
mso-border-bottom-themecolor:accent1;padding:0cm 0cm 4.0pt 0cm'>

<p class=MsoTitle><a name="_Toc352593053"></a><a name="_Toc351129868"><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc352593053'><span lang=EN-US>3. </span></span></a><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc352593053'><span lang=EN-US>Implementation</span></span></p>

</div>

<h1><a name="_Toc352593054"><span lang=EN-US>3.1<span style='mso-tab-count:
1'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Mobile Application</span></a></h1>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>This section will detail the implementation
of the mobile application that was developed using Android Studio IDE. The
application was developed in a modularized way so that each module served a
particular purpose.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The application has been built with
ÒMinimum SDK Version 15Ó and ÒTarget SDK Version 24Ó. The table below shows that
this means the application will be compatible with android platform version
4.0.3 up to version 7.0. [1] </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape

<h2><span lang=EN-US><span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;</span><a
name="_Toc352593055">3.1.1<span style='mso-tab-count:1'>&nbsp; </span>Application
Module</a></span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape
 id="_x0000_i1060" type="#_x0000_t75" alt="Description: Macintosh HD:Users:matthew:Desktop:Screenshots:Screen Shot 2017-03-25 at 22.10.01.png"
 style='width:229pt;height:73pt;visibility:visible;mso-wrap-style:square'
 o:bordertopcolor="black" o:borderleftcolor="black" o:borderbottomcolor="black"
 o:borderrightcolor="black">
 <v:imagedata src="TrackMe_Project_Report_files/image015.png" o:title="Screen Shot 2017-03-25 at 22.10.01.png"/>
 <w:bordertop type="single" width="6"/>
 <w:borderleft type="single" width="6"/>
 <w:borderbottom type="single" width="6"/>
 <w:borderright type="single" width="6"/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img width=231 height=75
src="TrackMe_Project_Report_files/image016.png"
alt="Description: Macintosh HD:Users:matthew:Desktop:Screenshots:Screen Shot 2017-03-25 at 22.10.01.png"
v:shapes="_x0000_i1060"><![endif]></span></p>

<p class=MsoCaption style='text-indent:36.0pt'><span lang=EN-US>Figure 3-1-2
Application Module</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>In order for the application to be able to
interact with the backend server I used AndroidÕs Volley Library. Volley is an HTTP
library that makes networking for Android apps easier and most importantly,
faster. [10]</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The application module sets up the core
Volley objects, such as the Volley request queue, and URLS needed to store user
location.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The Volley request queue is a handler for
request objects.</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:14.0pt;line-height:
150%;font-family:Roboto-Regular;mso-bidi-font-family:Roboto-Regular'> </span><span
lang=EN-US>It manages worker threads for running the network operations,
reading from and writing to the cache and parsing responses. [11]</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape
 id="_x0000_i1059" type="#_x0000_t75" alt="Description: Macintosh HD:Users:matthew:Desktop:Screenshots:Screen Shot 2017-03-25 at 19.44.31.png"
 style='width:415pt;height:50pt;visibility:visible;mso-wrap-style:square'

 o:borderbottomcolor="yellow pure" o:borderrightcolor="yellow pure">
 <v:imagedata src="TrackMe_Project_Report_files/image017.png" o:title="Screen Shot 2017-03-25 at 19.44.31.png"/>
 <w:bordertop type="single" width="6"/>
 <w:borderleft type="single" width="6"/>
 <w:borderbottom type="single" width="6"/>
 <w:borderright type="single" width="6"/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img width=417 height=52
src="TrackMe_Project_Report_files/image018.png"
alt="Description: Macintosh HD:Users:matthew:Desktop:Screenshots:Screen Shot 2017-03-25 at 19.44.31.png"
v:shapes="_x0000_i1059"><![endif]></span></p>

<p class=MsoCaption align=center style='text-align:center'><span lang=EN-US>Figure
3&#8209;1-3 AppConfig.java</span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc352593056"><span lang=EN-US>3.1.2<span style='mso-tab-count:
1'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Activity Module</span></a></h2>

<h2><span lang=EN-US style='mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape id="_x0000_i1058"
 type="#_x0000_t75" alt="Description: Macintosh HD:Users:matthew:Desktop:Screenshots:Screen Shot 2017-03-25 at 23.42.02.png"

 <w:bordertop type="single" width="6"/>
 <w:borderleft type="single" width="6"/>
 <w:borderbottom type="single" width="6"/>
 <w:borderright type="single" width="6"/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img width=228 height=99
src="TrackMe_Project_Report_files/image020.png"
alt="Description: Macintosh HD:Users:matthew:Desktop:Screenshots:Screen Shot 2017-03-25 at 23.42.02.png"
v:shapes="_x0000_i1058"><![endif]></span></h2>

<p class=MsoCaption><span lang=EN-US><span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span>Figure 3-1-4 Activity Module</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The activity module of the application was
built to handle fragment transaction &amp; the application navigation drawers.
The application navigation drawer allows the user to access the application
features such as login, registration, home screen &amp; preferences screen.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc352593057"><span lang=EN-US>Splash</span></a></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The Splash activity implements the
applicationsÕ splash screen. A splash screen is a screen usually seen upon app
start up that displays branding for the application. It is implemented in order
to give the application time to start up.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The splash screen implemented for TrackMe
is displayed for 5 seconds.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>This class queries if the user device has
location services turned on and if not it asks the user to enable location
services as theyÕre vital to the functionality of this application. If Location
Services are enabled this class proceeds to check is a user login session is
active using the <i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>SessionManager</i>
(Detailed later). If there is a login session active the <i style='mso-bidi-font-style:
normal'>MainActivity</i> is initiated and if not the <i style='mso-bidi-font-style:
normal'>StartupActivity</i> is initiated.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape
 id="_x0000_i1057" type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:154pt;height:199pt;
 visibility:visible;mso-wrap-style:square' o:bordertopcolor="black"
 o:borderleftcolor="black" o:borderbottomcolor="black" o:borderrightcolor="black">

 <w:borderleft type="single" width="6"/>
 <w:borderbottom type="single" width="6"/>
 <w:borderright type="single" width="6"/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img width=156 height=201
src="TrackMe_Project_Report_files/image022.png" v:shapes="_x0000_i1057"><![endif]></span><span
lang=EN-US><span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;</span><span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span
style='mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape id="_x0000_i1056" type="#_x0000_t75"

<p class=MsoCaption><span lang=EN-US><span

</span>Figure 3-1-5 Splash Screen<span style='mso-tab-count:4'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>
Figure 3&#8209;1-6 Location Services Request</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc352593058"><span lang=EN-US>StartupActivity</span></a></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The <i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>StartupActivity</i>
class hosts the Login &amp; Registration fragments as well providing access to
the About &amp; Help Fragments. This activity also hosts the startup navigation
drawer which allows the user to navigate between the available fragments. This
activity uses the local database handler class to query if a database for
TrackMe exists on the user device. If there is an existing database it is
assumed that the user has already registered an account so the user is
navigated to the login page, if not the user is navigated to the registration
page.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:108.0pt;page-break-after:avoid'><span
lang=EN-US><span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span
style='mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape id="Picture_x0020_4"
 o:spid="_x0000_i1055" type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:176pt;height:179pt;
 visibility:visible;mso-wrap-style:square' o:bordertopcolor="black"
 o:borderleftcolor="black" o:borderbottomcolor="black" o:borderrightcolor="black">
 <v:imagedata src="TrackMe_Project_Report_files/image025.png" o:title=""
  croptop="1f" cropbottom="28048f"/>
 <w:bordertop type="single" width="6"/>
 <w:borderleft type="single" width="6"/>
 <w:borderbottom type="single" width="6"/>
 <w:borderright type="single" width="6"/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img width=178 height=181
src="TrackMe_Project_Report_files/image026.png" v:shapes="Picture_x0020_4"><![endif]></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoCaption align=center style='text-align:center'><span lang=EN-US><span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Figure 3&#8209;1-7
StartupActivity Navigation Drawer</span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc352593059"><span lang=EN-US>MainActivity</span></a></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The <i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>MainActivity</i>
class hosts the applications main navigation drawer as well as handling the
navigation between all of the fragments that control the main features of the
app. </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The main activity also handles the
notification that is created when the application detects a possible fall. This
activity receives, through the implementation of a broadcast receiver, the
countdown timer information from a broadcast sent from the fall detection
service. If the stop button on the notification is not clicked before the time
runs out a text is sent to the users emergency contact letting them know that
the user may just have fallen.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:108.0pt;page-break-after:avoid'><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape id="Picture_x0020_3"
 o:spid="_x0000_i1054" type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:215pt;height:276pt;

  croptop="-1f" cropbottom="18148f"/>

 <w:borderbottom type="single" width="6"/>
 <w:borderright type="single" width="6"/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img width=217 height=278
src="TrackMe_Project_Report_files/image028.png" v:shapes="Picture_x0020_3"><![endif]></span></p>

<p class=MsoCaption align=center style='text-align:center'><span lang=EN-US>Figure
3&#8209;1-8 MainActivity Navigation Drawer</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:72.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape id="Picture_x0020_13"

<p class=MsoCaption align=center style='text-align:center'><span lang=EN-US>Figure

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc352593060"><span lang=EN-US>MyPreferenceActivity</span></a></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>This activity hosts the application
preferences fragment where the user can specify their preferences &amp;
settings for the following:</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='margin-left:72.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l7 level1 lfo16'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Fall Detection Enable</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:72.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l7 level1 lfo16'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>GPS Boundary Existing</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:72.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l7 level1 lfo16'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Emergency Contact Phone Number</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:72.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l7 level1 lfo16'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Notification Timer</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='margin-left:72.0pt;mso-add-space:auto;
text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l7 level1 lfo16'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Location Update Frequency</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The preference fragment automatically
implements handling of shared preferences so when a user changes a preference
it is automatically changed in the applications <i style='mso-bidi-font-style:
normal'>SharedPreference</i> file. This class automatically loads shared
preferences based on the user profile type (i.e. Default, Teenager, Adult or
Elderly).</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:108.0pt;page-break-after:avoid'><span
lang=EN-US><span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span
style='mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape id="Picture_x0020_2"

</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img width=210 height=216

<p class=MsoCaption style='margin-left:180.0pt'><span lang=EN-US>Figure 3&#8209;1-10
Preferences</span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc352593061"><span lang=EN-US>3.1.2<span style='mso-tab-count:
1'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Fragment Module</span></a></h2>

<h2><span lang=EN-US style='mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape id="Picture_x0020_37"

<p class=MsoCaption><span lang=EN-US><span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span>Figure
3-1-11 Fragment Module</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The fragment module of the application consists
of all of the fragment classes that formulate the main UI features of the
application. These fragments and their interactions are managed by the
applications activities.</span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc352593062"><span lang=EN-US style='mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:"\FF2D\FF33 \FF30\30B4\30B7\30C3\30AF";
mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:
minor-latin;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-bidi;
color:windowtext;font-weight:normal'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></a></h3>

<h3><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc352593062'><span lang=EN-US>HomeFragment</span></span></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The applications <i style='mso-bidi-font-style:
normal'>HomeFragment</i> class is the first fragment loaded upon successful user
login. This class queries the permission status of the necessary device
features that the application needs access to. On the occasion that the user
has not yet granted the necessary permissions to the application this activity
will request the user to grant permissions.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='page-break-after:avoid'><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape id="Picture_x0020_11"
 o:spid="_x0000_i1050" type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:177pt;height:201pt;

 <w:borderbottom type="single" width="6"/>
 <w:borderright type="single" width="6"/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img width=179 height=203
src="TrackMe_Project_Report_files/image036.png" v:shapes="Picture_x0020_11"><![endif]></span><span
lang=EN-US><span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span><span style='mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape id="Picture_x0020_12"

<p class=MsoCaption><span lang=EN-US>Figure 3&#8209;1-12 Location Permission<span
style='mso-tab-count:1'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style='mso-tab-count:

style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Figure 3&#8209;1-13
SMS Permission</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>This fragment hosts a Google Maps API <i
style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>SupportMapFragment</i> that displays the
current user location. If the GPS tracking service is running it will broadcast
an intent that is received by this fragment and the UI is updated to display a
marker at the latest user location.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:108.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape id="Picture_x0020_14"

 <w:borderright type="single" width="6"/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img width=200 height=280
src="TrackMe_Project_Report_files/image040.png" v:shapes="Picture_x0020_14"><![endif]></span></p>

<p class=MsoCaption align=center style='text-align:center'><span lang=EN-US>Figure
3&#8209;1-14 HomeFragment</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>This fragment provides buttons that allow
the user to start/stop the GPS tracking service, the service that tracks their
location, and to allow the user to track another users latest location update
to the cloud server by entering their username.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:108.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape id="Picture_x0020_15"

<p class=MsoCaption align=center style='text-align:center'><span lang=EN-US>Figure
3&#8209;1-15 Tracking A User<span style='mso-no-proof:yes'><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc352593063"><span lang=EN-US>TrackUserFragment</span></a></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>Upon the successful request for the latest
location update of a user in the <i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>HomeFragment</i>
the <i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>TrackUserFragment</i> is opened and
it displays the users latest location and the time at which that location
update was posted to the backend server. The location update is retrieved using
the Cloud Database Handler class.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape
 id="Picture_x0020_19" o:spid="_x0000_i1046" type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:414pt;

</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img width=416 height=172
src="TrackMe_Project_Report_files/image044.png" v:shapes="Picture_x0020_19"><![endif]></span></p>

<p class=MsoCaption align=center style='text-align:center'><span lang=EN-US>Figure
3&#8209;1-16 Remotely Viewing User Location<span style='mso-no-proof:yes'><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc352593064"><span lang=EN-US>RegisterFragment</span></a></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The <i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>RegisterFragment</i>
class allows the user to create a TrackMe account and post their details to the
TrackMe backend server.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>This fragment allows the user to enter the
following details:</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l16 level1 lfo17'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Name</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l16 level1 lfo17'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Email</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l16 level1 lfo17'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Username</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l16 level1 lfo17'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Phone Number</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l16 level1 lfo17'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Password + Confirmation</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l16 level1 lfo17'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Profile Type</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The fragment implements a Volley post
request and posts the users details server side database interaction
application that in turn posts the data to the TrackMe backend server. This
fragment runs error some checking making sure that the fundamental profile
details are entered by the user (i.e. Name, Email, Username, Password). If the
user has not entered all mandatory details the application will prompt the user
to enter the missing information. [1]</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:108.0pt'><span lang=EN-US><span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style='mso-no-proof:
yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape id="_x0000_i1045" type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:169pt;
 height:266pt;visibility:visible;mso-wrap-style:square' o:bordertopcolor="black"
 o:borderleftcolor="black" o:borderbottomcolor="black" o:borderrightcolor="black">
 <v:imagedata src="TrackMe_Project_Report_files/image045.png" o:title=""
  croptop="3580f" cropbottom="3907f"/>
 <w:bordertop type="single" width="6"/>
 <w:borderleft type="single" width="6"/>
 <w:borderbottom type="single" width="6"/>
 <w:borderright type="single" width="6"/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img width=171 height=268
src="TrackMe_Project_Report_files/image046.png" v:shapes="_x0000_i1045"><![endif]></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoCaption align=center style='text-align:center'><span lang=EN-US>Figure
3&#8209;1-17 Register Fragment UI</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc352593065"><span lang=EN-US>LoginFragment</span></a></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The <i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>LoginFragment</i>
class allows the user to log in to their TrackMe account. This fragment uses a
volley post request to post the login details entered by the user to the server
side database interaction application.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>Since the application requires Internet
access to function at itÕs highest capacity &amp; connect to the backend cloud
database this fragment will only allow a user to login if thereÕs an Internet
connection available on their device. [1]</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:108.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape id="Picture_x0020_22"
 o:spid="_x0000_i1044" type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:205pt;height:235pt;

 o:borderleftcolor="yellow pure" o:borderbottomcolor="yellow pure"
 o:borderrightcolor="yellow pure">
 <v:imagedata src="TrackMe_Project_Report_files/image047.png" o:title=""
  croptop="2943f" cropbottom="31601f"/>
 <w:bordertop type="single" width="6"/>
 <w:borderleft type="single" width="6"/>
 <w:borderbottom type="single" width="6"/>
 <w:borderright type="single" width="6"/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img width=207 height=237
src="TrackMe_Project_Report_files/image048.png" v:shapes="Picture_x0020_22"><![endif]></span></p>

<p class=MsoCaption align=center style='text-align:center'><span lang=EN-US>Figure
3&#8209;1-18 Login Fragment UI</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc352593066"><span lang=EN-US>AboutFragment</span></a></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>This fragment displays some information
about the application to the user. It provides information such as the goals of
the application and the applicationsÕ features.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:108.0pt;page-break-after:avoid'><span

<h3><a name="_Toc352593067"><span lang=EN-US>HelpFragment</span></a></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:115%'><span lang=EN-US>This fragment
displays some information about the application settings. </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:115%'><span lang=EN-US>It also offers
configuration guidelines for these user settings.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:108.0pt;line-height:115%;page-break-after:
avoid'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape
 id="Picture_x0020_6" o:spid="_x0000_i1042" type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:180pt;

<p class=MsoCaption align=center style='text-align:center'><span lang=EN-US>Figure
3&#8209;1-20 HelpFragment</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc352593068"><span lang=EN-US>ProfileFragment</span></a></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>This fragment displays user profile
details. These details include items such as a users phone number, email,
username, first name and surname.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>It has a private inner class that acts as an
adapter to display the <i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>hashmap</i>
entries in a <i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>ListView</i> object. This
adapter takes in a <i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>hashmap</i> as a
parameter and puts itsÕ entries into the <i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>ListView</i>
object specified in the fragments layout xml file.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:108.0pt;page-break-after:avoid'><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape id="_x0000_i1041"
 type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:188pt;height:200pt;visibility:visible;

 o:borderbottomcolor="yellow pure" o:borderrightcolor="yellow pure">

  cropbottom="26292f"/>
 <w:bordertop type="single" width="6"/>
 <w:borderleft type="single" width="6"/>
