 <w:borderright type="single" width="6"/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img width=190 height=202
src="TrackMe_Project_Report_files/image054.png" v:shapes="_x0000_i1041"><![endif]></span></p>

<p class=MsoCaption align=center style='text-align:center'><span lang=EN-US>Figure
3-1-21 ProfileFragment</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc352593069"><span lang=EN-US>3.1.3<span style='mso-tab-count:
1'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Services Module</span></a></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The services module contains the Service classes
that provide the applications fundamental features i.e. GPS Location Tracking
and Fall Detection.</span></p>

<h2><span lang=EN-US style='mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape id="Picture_x0020_9"
 o:spid="_x0000_i1040" type="#_x0000_t75" alt="Description: Macintosh HD:Users:matthew:Desktop:Screenshots:Screen Shot 2017-03-25 at 22.19.27.png"
 style='width:199pt;height:61pt;visibility:visible;mso-wrap-style:square'
 o:bordertopcolor="black" o:borderleftcolor="black" o:borderbottomcolor="black"
 o:borderrightcolor="black">
 <v:imagedata src="TrackMe_Project_Report_files/image055.png" o:title="Screen Shot 2017-03-25 at 22.19.27.png"/>
 <w:bordertop type="single" width="6"/>
 <w:borderleft type="single" width="6"/>
 <w:borderbottom type="single" width="6"/>
 <w:borderright type="single" width="6"/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img width=201 height=63
src="TrackMe_Project_Report_files/image056.png"
alt="Description: Macintosh HD:Users:matthew:Desktop:Screenshots:Screen Shot 2017-03-25 at 22.19.27.png"
v:shapes="Picture_x0020_9"><![endif]></span></h2>

<p class=MsoCaption><span lang=EN-US>Figure 3&#8209;1-22 Services Module</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc352593070"><span lang=EN-US>GPS Service</span></a></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The GPS service implements an Android
Location listener. It is configurable to query location at a user specified
interval with the default interval being 60 seconds. The GPS service is set up
so that it uses the most accurate location data available at all times. </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape
 id="Picture_x0020_27" o:spid="_x0000_i1039" type="#_x0000_t75" alt="Description: Macintosh HD:Users:matthew:Desktop:Screenshots:Screen Shot 2017-03-26 at 03.26.08.png"
 style='width:415pt;height:255pt;visibility:visible;mso-wrap-style:square'>
 <v:imagedata src="TrackMe_Project_Report_files/image057.png" o:title="Screen Shot 2017-03-26 at 03.26.08.png"/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img width=417 height=257
src="TrackMe_Project_Report_files/image058.png"
alt="Description: Macintosh HD:Users:matthew:Desktop:Screenshots:Screen Shot 2017-03-26 at 03.26.08.png"
v:shapes="Picture_x0020_27"><![endif]></span></p>

<p class=MsoCaption align=center style='text-align:center'><span lang=EN-US>Figure
3&#8209;1-23 GPS Location Service</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>When this service is started a <i
style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>LatLng</i> object is initialized so that the
user starting location is saved. This initial location object is used to check
if the user has travelled outside the specified boundary from their starting
point.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>When a location update is obtained this
service updates both the local SQLite database and the MySQL cloud database (if
the user device is connected to the Internet) with the users latest location
details</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>Upon each location update the algorithm runs
verifications to check whether the user has travelled outside of a specified
boundary distance from their starting location. If the user has travelled
outside the specified boundary then an SMS is sent to their emergency contact with
their latest location details.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape
 id="Picture_x0020_26" o:spid="_x0000_i1038" type="#_x0000_t75" alt="Description: Macintosh HD:Users:matthew:Desktop:Screenshots:Screen Shot 2017-03-26 at 03.24.48.png"
 style='width:396pt;height:147pt;visibility:visible;mso-wrap-style:square'>
 <v:imagedata src="TrackMe_Project_Report_files/image059.png" o:title="Screen Shot 2017-03-26 at 03.24.48.png"/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img width=398 height=149
src="TrackMe_Project_Report_files/image060.png"
alt="Description: Macintosh HD:Users:matthew:Desktop:Screenshots:Screen Shot 2017-03-26 at 03.24.48.png"
v:shapes="Picture_x0020_26"><![endif]></span></p>

<p class=MsoCaption align=center style='text-align:center'><span lang=EN-US>Figure
3&#8209;1-24 GPS Boundary Check</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc352593071"><span lang=EN-US>Fall Detection Service</span></a></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The fall detection service is a fundamental
application feature. This class runs a background servicer that implements a
sensor event listener that is used to process readings from the device
accelerometer. </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>Each time a sensor reading is processed this
service computes the reading using Euclidean vector mathematics to see if the
characteristics of the reading are deemed to be a possible fall. [16]</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The criteria specified for a fall are that
the accelerometer value had spiked above 25m/s or below 1m/s bearing in mind
that at a standstill the computed reading would be approximately 9.8m/s
accounting for natural gravitational pull. If these criteria are met then fall
detection service deems the readings to constitute a possible fall. A timer is then
started and an intent containing the timerÕs readings is broadcast. If the
timer reaches 0 without being cancelled by the user (through the main activity
notification created) then an SMS is sent to the users emergency contact
letting them know that a possible fall may have occurred.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The timers default value is set to 30
seconds but is user configurable through the application preferences.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape
 id="Picture_x0020_28" o:spid="_x0000_i1037" type="#_x0000_t75" alt="Description: Macintosh HD:Users:matthew:Desktop:Screenshots:Screen Shot 2017-03-26 at 03.29.23.png"
 style='width:415pt;height:159pt;visibility:visible;mso-wrap-style:square'
 o:bordertopcolor="black" o:borderleftcolor="black" o:borderbottomcolor="black"
 o:borderrightcolor="black">
 <v:imagedata src="TrackMe_Project_Report_files/image061.png" o:title="Screen Shot 2017-03-26 at 03.29.23.png"/>
 <w:bordertop type="single" width="6"/>
 <w:borderleft type="single" width="6"/>
 <w:borderbottom type="single" width="6"/>
 <w:borderright type="single" width="6"/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img width=417 height=161
src="TrackMe_Project_Report_files/image062.png"
alt="Description: Macintosh HD:Users:matthew:Desktop:Screenshots:Screen Shot 2017-03-26 at 03.29.23.png"
v:shapes="Picture_x0020_28"><![endif]></span></p>

<p class=MsoCaption align=center style='text-align:center'><span lang=EN-US>Figure
3&#8209;1-25 Fall Detection</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc352593072"><span lang=EN-US>3.1.4<span style='mso-tab-count:
1'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Helper Module</span></a></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The Helper module provides utilities to
enhance the functionality of other classes in the application.</span></p>

<h2><span lang=EN-US style='mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape id="Picture_x0020_10"
 o:spid="_x0000_i1036" type="#_x0000_t75" alt="Description: Macintosh HD:Users:matthew:Desktop:Screenshots:Screen Shot 2017-03-25 at 22.19.19.png"
 style='width:211pt;height:136pt;visibility:visible;mso-wrap-style:square'>
 <v:imagedata src="TrackMe_Project_Report_files/image063.png" o:title="Screen Shot 2017-03-25 at 22.19.19.png"/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img width=213 height=138
src="TrackMe_Project_Report_files/image064.png"
alt="Description: Macintosh HD:Users:matthew:Desktop:Screenshots:Screen Shot 2017-03-25 at 22.19.19.png"
v:shapes="Picture_x0020_10"><![endif]></span></h2>

<p class=MsoCaption style='margin-left:36.0pt'><span lang=EN-US><span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Figure
3-1-26 Helper Module</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc352593073"><span lang=EN-US>CloudDBHandler</span></a></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The <i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>CloudDBHandler</i>
class handles user location data HTTP GET and POST requests to the Cloud
database. This includes posting of users location data to the cloud database as
well as querying a users latest location update. To achieve this functionality
this class uses Android Volley objects to manage GET and POST requests.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc352593074"><span lang=EN-US>GPSHelper</span></a></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The <i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>GPSHelper</i>
class provides utilities to help augment the GPS location tracking functionality.
These utilities include retrieval of address Strings using a Geocoder (If an
internet connection is available on the device). This class also implements a <i
style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>LocationListener</i> so that the users
location can be retrieved upon app startup</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc352593075"><span lang=EN-US>LocalDBHandler</span></a></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The <i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>LocalDBHandler</i>
class provides utilities to manage the local devices SQLite database. Upon the
initial application install and startup this class creates the local SQLite
database and initializes the ÔuserÕ and ÔlocationÕ tables within this database.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The ÔuserÕ table contains user profile
details for any user that logs into the TrackMe application on that device.
These details include name, username, email, profile type, ID and unique ID.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The ÔlocationÕ table contains user location
details that are generated when running the applications GPS tracking service.
These details include id, username, latitude value, longitude value, unique ID
and a timestamp relating to when the location data was obtained.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The devices manages the size of the user ÔlocationÕ
table using an SQL trigger that limits the size of the table to 50 rows so that
the impact of the table on available device storage is limited.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>This class also handles database upgrade so
when the application is upgraded any existing database is deleted and a new
database containing empty ÔuserÕ and ÔlocationÕ tables is created.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc352593076"><span lang=EN-US>MessageHandler</span></a></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The <i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>MessageHandler</i>
class handles the transmission of SMS messages to the users specified emergency
contact. The message to be sent is taken in as an argument as the message
content is specific to the scenario detected by the application (i.e. Messages
sent for fall detection differ to messages sent for boundary detection).</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc352593077"><span lang=EN-US>SessionManager</span></a></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The <i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>SessionManager</i>
class handles the creation and termination of user login sessions. This
involves the setting of shared preferences for the logged in user (i.e. Setting
their profile details as the shared preferences) and the deletion of these
shared preferences from device storage upon a user logging out. [2]<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span>This
class contains getter and setter methods for all possible shared preferences.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc352593078"><span lang=EN-US>WidgetHandler</span></a></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>This class defines the functionality of the
TrackMe application widget from which the user can start or stop the GPS
tracking service as well as being able to start the application or opening the
existing instance of the application if it has already been started.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:72.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape id="Picture_x0020_1"
 o:spid="_x0000_i1035" type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:262pt;height:3in;
 visibility:visible;mso-wrap-style:square'>
 <v:imagedata src="TrackMe_Project_Report_files/image065.png" o:title=""
  croptop="9427f" cropbottom="24069f" cropleft="1f" cropright="-1478f"/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img width=264 height=218
src="TrackMe_Project_Report_files/image066.png" v:shapes="Picture_x0020_1"><![endif]></span></p>

<p class=MsoCaption align=center style='text-align:center'><span lang=EN-US>Figure
3&#8209;1-27 TrackMe Widget</span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc352593079"><span lang=EN-US>3.1.5<span style='mso-tab-count:
1'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>UI</span></a></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The applications UI was designed to be
user-friendly with ease of use being the primary objective behind the design
features. The application allows navigation between pages by utilizing
navigation drawers and the Android OSÕs native back button.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp; </span>The applications UI theme is a simple
theme that uses black, white and turquoise throughout.</span></p>

<h1><a name="_Toc352593084"><span lang=EN-US>3.2<span style='mso-tab-count:
1'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Server-Side Project</span></a></h1>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The <i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>TrackMeServer</i>
PHP project, which is hosted on NUI GalwayÕs Danu6 server, handles the mobile
applications interactions with the MySQL cloud database.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape

</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img width=417 height=73

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc352593085"><span lang=EN-US>DBFn</span></a></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The <i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>DBFn</i>
class contains all the database functions needed by the mobile application to
interact with the cloud database. </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>This class contains all the SQL queries
needed by the application for user registration, login, location updates &amp;
location queries.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>It provides error checking for user detail
duplication such as username, email and password. If any of these database
column entries already exists in the user details table, in the cloud database,
when a new user is registering an account this class echoes a JSON response to
the user device informing them of the duplication details.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>This class provides functionality to insert
user details into the cloud database.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape
 id="Picture_x0020_23" o:spid="_x0000_i1030" type="#_x0000_t75" alt="Description: Macintosh HD:Users:matthew:Desktop:Screenshots:Screen Shot 2017-03-26 at 15.46.40.png"
 style='width:463pt;height:29pt;visibility:visible;mso-wrap-style:square'>
 <v:imagedata src="TrackMe_Project_Report_files/image075.png" o:title="Screen Shot 2017-03-26 at 15.46.40.png"/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img width=465 height=31
src="TrackMe_Project_Report_files/image076.png"
alt="Description: Macintosh HD:Users:matthew:Desktop:Screenshots:Screen Shot 2017-03-26 at 15.46.40.png"
v:shapes="Picture_x0020_23"><![endif]></span></p>

<p class=MsoCaption align=center style='text-align:center'><a
name="_Toc352537138"></a><a name="_Toc352536924"></a><a name="_Toc352534270"></a><a
name="_Toc352533889"><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc352534270'><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc352536924'><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc352537138'><span
lang=EN-US>Figure 3&#8209;2&#8209;</span></span></span></span></a><!--[if supportFields]><span

style='mso-bookmark:_Toc352536924'><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc352537138'></span></span></span></span><span
style='mso-element:field-end'></span><![endif]--><span style='mso-bookmark:
_Toc352533889'><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc352534270'><span style='mso-bookmark:
_Toc352536924'><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc352537138'><span lang=EN-US>
Saving User Details</span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>Prior to user details being posted to the
cloud database the users password is encrypted using a hash/salt mechanism.
This provides a more secure user login implementation meaning that even if the
raw database were to be compromised user details would be unobtainable. [1]</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape
 id="Picture_x0020_29" o:spid="_x0000_i1029" type="#_x0000_t75" alt="Description: Macintosh HD:Users:matthew:Desktop:Screenshots:Screen Shot 2017-03-26 at 15.48.10.png"
 style='width:415pt;height:88pt;visibility:visible;mso-wrap-style:square'>
 <v:imagedata src="TrackMe_Project_Report_files/image077.png" o:title="Screen Shot 2017-03-26 at 15.48.10.png"/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img width=417 height=90
src="TrackMe_Project_Report_files/image078.png"
alt="Description: Macintosh HD:Users:matthew:Desktop:Screenshots:Screen Shot 2017-03-26 at 15.48.10.png"
v:shapes="Picture_x0020_29"><![endif]></span></p>

<p class=MsoCaption align=center style='text-align:center'><a
name="_Toc352534271"></a><a name="_Toc352533890"><span style='mso-bookmark:
_Toc352534271'><span lang=EN-US>Figure 3&#8209;2&#8209;3 Hash Function</span></span></a></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>User location details can be posted to the
server using this class. This class provides functionality that posts location
details to 2 different tables in the cloud database. </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>One table contains all location updates for
every user whereas the other contains one entry for each user that has posted
location updates. This single entry per user corresponds to the users latest
location update that has been posted to the cloud database.</span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc352593086"><span lang=EN-US>DBConfig</span></a></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>This class defines the parameters needed to
make a connection to the cloud database. The parameters are the following:</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l12 level1 lfo18'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Database Host</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l12 level1 lfo18'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Database User</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l12 level1 lfo18'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>User Password</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l12 level1 lfo18'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Database Name</span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc352593087"><span lang=EN-US>DBConnect</span></a></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>This class contains one method that uses
the database details configured in the <i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>DBConfig</i>
class to connect to the cloud database.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>If the connection is successful this class
returns the connection object.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>If not, this class echoes response saying
that a database connection was unable to be established.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape
 id="Picture_x0020_30" o:spid="_x0000_i1028" type="#_x0000_t75" alt="Description: Macintosh HD:Users:matthew:Desktop:Screenshots:Screen Shot 2017-03-26 at 15.59.52.png"

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc352593088"><span lang=EN-US>Register</span></a></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>This class handles user registration HTTP
POST requests.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>It runs some error checking to see if a
user is attempting to register using an already occupied email address,
username or phone number.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>If there isnÕt any duplication in the
request details then a <i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>DBFn</i> object
method is called to save the user details. </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>Upon successful registration of user
details this class returns a JSON Object containing the users details and if
user registration is unsuccessful a JSON object containing some error
information is returned to the user device.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape
 id="Picture_x0020_31" o:spid="_x0000_i1027" type="#_x0000_t75" alt="Description: Macintosh HD:Users:matthew:Desktop:Screenshots:Screen Shot 2017-03-26 at 16.26.39.png"

</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img width=389 height=168
src="TrackMe_Project_Report_files/image082.png"
alt="Description: Macintosh HD:Users:matthew:Desktop:Screenshots:Screen Shot 2017-03-26 at 16.26.39.png"
v:shapes="Picture_x0020_31"><![endif]></span></p>

<p class=MsoCaption align=center style='text-align:center'><a
name="_Toc352537140"></a><a name="_Toc352536926"></a><a name="_Toc352534273"></a><a

style='mso-bookmark:_Toc352536926'><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc352537140'><span
lang=EN-US>Figure 3&#8209;2&#8209;5 Registration</span></span></span></span></a></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc352593089"><span lang=EN-US>Login</span></a></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>This class handlers user login HTTP POST
requests received from the mobile application. If verifies the user details
entered using a <i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>DBFn </i>object method.
If the details are deemed to be correct this class returns the user details in
a JSON response object.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>If the user enters incorrect details an
error is flagged and JSON response containing an error message is sent back to
the user device containing the error details.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:108.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape id="Picture_x0020_32"

src="TrackMe_Project_Report_files/image084.png"

v:shapes="Picture_x0020_32"><![endif]></span></p>

<p class=MsoCaption align=center style='text-align:center'><a
name="_Toc352537141"></a><a name="_Toc352536927"></a><a name="_Toc352534274"></a><a

lang=EN-US>Figure 3-2&#8209;6 Login</span></span></span></span></a></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc352593090"><span lang=EN-US>UpdateLocation</span></a></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The <i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>UpdateLocation</i>
class handles user location updates received from the mobile application. It
receives these HTTP POST request containing the users own details along with
their location details. It proceeds to call the <i style='mso-bidi-font-style:
normal'>saveUserLocation</i> method in the <i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>DBFn</i>
class (functionality of which detailed above) to store the information in the
cloud database.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc352593091"><span lang=EN-US>GetLocation</span></a></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The <i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>GetLocation</i>
class handles user location queries.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>It receives POST requests from the mobile
application with the username to query the latest location data for.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>This class then proceeds to call the <i
style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>getUserLocation</i> method in the <i
style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>DBFn</i> class (functionality of which
detailed above)</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>Upon successful retrieval of a users
location data the method returns the location details in a JSON response</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h1><a name="_Toc352593092"><span lang=EN-US>3.3<span style='mso-tab-count:
1'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Database</span></a></h1>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>This section details the schemas used in
the MySQL cloud database.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>This database consists of 3 tables used by
the mobile application:</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l23 level1 lfo19'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>á<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span
lang=EN-US>userDetails<o:p></o:p></span></i></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l23 level1 lfo19'><![if !supportLists]><span

</span></span></span><![endif]><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span
lang=EN-US>usersLocations<o:p></o:p></span></i></p>

</span></span></span><![endif]><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span
lang=EN-US>latestUserLocation<o:p></o:p></span></i></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape
 id="Picture_x0020_34" o:spid="_x0000_i1025" type="#_x0000_t75" alt="Description: Macintosh HD:Users:matthew:Desktop:Screenshots:Screen Shot 2017-03-26 at 16.40.15.png"

<p class=MsoCaption align=center style='text-align:center'><span lang=EN-US>3&#8209;3-1
Cloud Database Schemas</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The <i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>userDetails</i>
table uses <i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>id</i> (an auto incrementing
integer value) as itÕs primary key with <i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>unique_id</i>,
<i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>email, username and phone_no</i> being indexes
in the table.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The <i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>usersLocations</i>
table uses <i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>timestamp</i> as itÕs primary
key with <i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>unique_id</i> being an index in
the table.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The <i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>latestUserLocation</i>
table uses the <i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>unique_id</i> field as
itÕs primary key with <i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>username</i> acting
as its index.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<div style='mso-element:para-border-div;border:none;border-bottom:solid #4F81BD 1.0pt;
mso-border-bottom-themecolor:accent1;padding:0cm 0cm 4.0pt 0cm'>

<p class=MsoTitle><a name="_Toc352593093"><span lang=EN-US>4. Testing &amp; Evaluation</span></a><span
lang=EN-US> </span></p>

</div>

<h1><a name="_Toc352593094"><span lang=EN-US>4.1<span style='mso-tab-count:
1'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Testing</span></a><span lang=EN-US> </span></h1>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>This section gives an overview of the
testing completed throughout the course of the applications development. The
majority of the testing was carried out on a Motorola G4 Plus smartphone device
running Android version 6.0.1 (API 23).<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span><span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span>Other
devices used to test the application were an LG G4, a OnePlus Three, a Sony
Xperia Z3 and the Android Studio IDEÕs inbuilt emulator. All devices used to
test were running Android versions between 4.0.3 and 7.0.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc352593095"><span lang=EN-US>Testing Of GPS Tracking Algorithm</span></a></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>To test the GPS location algorithmsÕ
accuracy I started the tracking algorithms in multiple known locations where
the address was known to me so I could assess whether or not the location
address obtained from the Geocoder was accurate. </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>I found the location data received to be
very accurate as around 80% of the time the exact address location was obtained
(accuracy to the detail of the exact house number) and the rest of the time the
location data obtained was very close to the real location (Usually one house
number, or the equivalent, away from the actual location).</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>During the testing process of the GPS
boundary algorithm I used various different boundary settings. Each time I
started the GPS tracking algorithm when I was in the same location, I would
travel slightly beyond the approximate distance of the boundary variable I had
set and then test whether or not an ÔemergencyÕ message was sent to the
emergency contact that I had defined. The boundary tracking always proved to be
very accurate with the only real issue arising being the permissions needed to
send a background SMS, Once this was rectified the boundary tracking and SMS
sending worked flawlessly. </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The reliability of the algorithm was tested
by running several instances of the application, with the GPS Tracking service
running, over a long period of time. It was observed whether ach of these
instances tested location data was uploaded to the cloud database as expected.
This never proved to be an issue.</span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc352593096"><span lang=EN-US>Testing Of Fall Detection
Algorithm</span></a></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The fall detection algorithm was tested and
tuned over the period of a number of weeks. The application was reconfigured
and tuned several times with different characteristics defined that would
indicate a possible fall. Each time it was reconfigured I simulated a number of
accelerometer spikes that I would have either classified as falls or not.
Throughout the course of this testing I was able to identify the most accurate
parameters for fall detection so that the algorithm would be slightly
oversensitive. I decided to implement the algorithm in this way as personal
security is the fundamental aim of this application and because of that I would
rather detect a false positive rather than a false negative.</span></p>

<h1><a name="_Toc352593097"><span lang=EN-US>4.2<span style='mso-tab-count:
1'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>User Feedback</span></a></h1>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>Throughout the course of the development
process I deployed the application to a number of my friends and familyÕs Android
devices.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The application was deployed to user
devices in various stages of development to test a range of the applications
features such as fall detection, GPS tracking as well as UI interactions and
compatibility with various devices.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The versions of the application deployed to
user devices ranged from early version with very little background
functionality, so to allow users to test the application UI and
login/registration features of the application, to later versions of the
application deployed to user devices to allow them to test the accuracy of the
fall detection and GPS tracking.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>User feedback proved to be a very effective
method of discovering application functionality based bugs and changes that
needed to be implemented. This was due to the fact new users of the application
often carried out variating sequences of interaction with the app that I had
not anticipated. </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>This led to the discovery of several bugs
in the applications underlying functionality.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>Some bugs identified by users are as
follows:</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l13 level1 lfo24'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>1.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Email duplication upon
registration let to error and inability for application to continue.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l13 level1 lfo24'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>2.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Opening of application without
location services turned on led to application crash.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l13 level1 lfo24'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>3.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Emergency contact configuration
was not saved upon re-opening of the application.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l13 level1 lfo24'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>4.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>No functionality to check for
duplication of username of phone number was present in earlier versions of the
application.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>I also adopted user feedback as my main
source of UI testing as I felt that errors and bad practice in the applications
UI would be very easily picked up by first time users due to their impartial
and newly-formulated perspective of the application.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span><span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span>This method
helped identify several application UI bugs that I had not previously observed
as well as suggestions to improve that applications flow and ease of use. </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>This feedback led to the following changes
in the application:</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l10 level1 lfo25'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>1.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Change to using navigation
drawers to navigate through application.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l10 level1 lfo25'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>2.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>Placement of <i
style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>TrackMe</i> and <i style='mso-bidi-font-style:
normal'>Track Someone</i> button at the top of the <i style='mso-bidi-font-style:
normal'>HomeFragment</i> UI.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l10 level1 lfo25'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>3.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>The decision to include <i
style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>HelpFragment</i> and <i style='mso-bidi-font-style:
normal'>AboutFragment</i> in the application so users would have access to
guidelines for application configurations as well as being able to see a
summary of the features the application offered.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>Overall I found user feedback to be a very useful
and productive method of application testing.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>I found it useful for several reasons such
as:</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l8 level1 lfo26'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>1.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>New users offered a fresh
perspective on the application.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l8 level1 lfo26'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>2.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>New users oftentimes carried
out interactions of the application that I had not considered of previously
used leading to the discovery of bugs or the opportunity to add new features to
the application.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l8 level1 lfo26'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>3.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>New users often used the
application with device settings configurations that I had not considered or
tested leading to the discovery of bugs.</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h1><a name="_Toc352593098"><span lang=EN-US>4.3<span style='mso-tab-count:
1'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Functional Requirements Review</span></a></h1>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>This section reviews the functional
requirements set out in the original Software Requirements Specification for
the project. It details whether or not the requirements were completed and if
not the reasoning or rationale behind the decision or constraint.</span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc352593099"><span lang=EN-US>Core Requirements</span></a></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:
normal'><span lang=EN-US>FR1 - User Registration<o:p></o:p></span></i></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span lang=EN-US>Complete
As Defined. </span></i><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-family:Times;mso-bidi-font-family:Times'><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The application allows for users to
register an account for the TrackMe application. </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:
normal'><span lang=EN-US>FR2 - User Profile <o:p></o:p></span></i></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span lang=EN-US>Complete
As Defined.</span></i><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-family:Times;mso-bidi-font-family:Times'><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The application allows the user to
configure profile details and choose from various default profile types. </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:
normal'><span lang=EN-US>FR3 - Location Tracking<o:p></o:p></span></i></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span lang=EN-US>Complete
As Defined.</span></i><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-family:Times;mso-bidi-font-family:Times'><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The application has the ability to track a
users location at all times given that there is either network or internet
connection available on the user device.</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-family:Times;mso-bidi-font-family:Times'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:
normal'><span lang=EN-US>FR4 - TrackMe (Request To Be Tracked) <o:p></o:p></span></i></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span lang=EN-US>Incomplete
As Defined.</span></i><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-family:Times;mso-bidi-font-family:Times'><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The application sends an SMS to the users
defined emergency contact if a scenario is detected where the user might be in
danger. This SMS contains information such as their username and latest location
address. The username can be used to see a visual representation of the latest
location of the user.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:
normal'><span lang=EN-US>FR5 - Fall Detection <o:p></o:p></span></i></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span lang=EN-US>Complete
As Defined</span></i><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-family:Times;mso-bidi-font-family:Times'>.<o:p></o:p></span></i></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The application has the ability to detect a
user fall. </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>This service can also be enabled or
disabled depending on user preference.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:
normal'><span lang=EN-US>FR6 - Messaging Settings <o:p></o:p></span></i></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span lang=EN-US>Incomplete
as Defined<o:p></o:p></span></i></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The application has been defined so that it
uses SMS as itÕs messaging service as it is the only means of sending a message
that doesnÕt require any user interaction which was a fundamental requirement
of the applications messaging feature.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:
normal'><span lang=EN-US>FR7 - Contacts <o:p></o:p></span></i></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span lang=EN-US>Incomplete
As Defined.<o:p></o:p></span></i></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The application allows the selection of an
emergency contact that is sent an SMS upon the detection an <i
style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'>emergency</i> situation.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:
normal'><span lang=EN-US>FR8 - Help Menu <o:p></o:p></span></i></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span lang=EN-US>Complete
As Defined</span></i><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-family:Times;mso-bidi-font-family:Times'><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The user is given the ability to access
guidelines for configuring the application.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:
normal'><span lang=EN-US>FR9 - Push Notifications <o:p></o:p></span></i></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span lang=EN-US>Complete
As Defined</span></i><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-family:Times;mso-bidi-font-family:Times'><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The ability to show push notifications on
the Android OS home screen in the case of a fall being detected.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc352593100"><span lang=EN-US>Additional Requirements</span></a></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:
normal'><span lang=EN-US>FR10 - Social Media Account Integration <o:p></o:p></span></i></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span lang=EN-US>Incomplete
as defined</span></i><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-family:Times;mso-bidi-font-family:Times'><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>Due to time constraints and a change in
direction this wasnÕt seen as a fundamental requirement as social media
accounts wouldnÕt be used as a messaging service in the application.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:
normal'><span lang=EN-US>FR11 - DB Management Web Service <o:p></o:p></span></i></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span lang=EN-US>Incomplete
As Defined</span></i><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-family:Times;mso-bidi-font-family:Times'><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>Development of a web service to administer
the DB was not undertaken due to time constraints and requirement
prioritization.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:
normal'><span lang=EN-US>FR12 - Real Time Data Analytics <o:p></o:p></span></i></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span lang=EN-US>Incomplete
As Defined</span></i><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-family:Times;mso-bidi-font-family:Times'><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>Due to time constraints I was unable to
complete the implementation of a backend web service that ran data analytics on
the user location data uploaded to the backend server. </span></p>

<h1><a name="_Toc352593101"><span lang=EN-US>4.4<span style='mso-tab-count:
1'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Comparison With Similar Applications</span></a></h1>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The TrackMe performs admirably in terms of
available features in comparison to the other personal security applications researched
as part of this project.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The feature matrix below, that includes
similar applications, highlights that TrackMe provides many of the same
fundamental security features that are provided by professional subscription
based services. TrackMe also has the added ability of fall detection that gives
it another dimension in comparison to other similar products.</span></p>

<div style='mso-element:para-border-div;border:none;border-bottom:solid #4F81BD 1.0pt;
mso-border-bottom-themecolor:accent1;padding:0cm 0cm 4.0pt 0cm'>

<p class=MsoTitle><a name="_Toc352593102"><span lang=EN-US>5. Conclusion</span></a></p>

</div>

<h1><a name="_Toc352593103"><span lang=EN-US>5.1<span style='mso-tab-count:
1'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Project Outcome</span></a></h1>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>This project meets the primary goals of
developing a smartphone application that is used to aid the personal security
of vulnerable adults and children. The application enables periodic device
check-in, remote monitoring of device location, detection of lack of movement
(through the fall detection algorithm) and has the ability to detect user movement
outside specified boundaries depending on the requirements of the individual
being monitored. The smartphone application in enhanced by a backend server
that serves that purposes of making data available to other relevant users of
the application that can query the data.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>Overall I am happy with the experience I
have gained in Android Development that enhanced my ability to built smartphone
application as well as enhancing my competency in Java programming.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The completion of the project also gave my
good experience in using PHP and learning about the fundamentals database administration.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>I believe that the skills IÕve learned due
to competing this project will be of great benefit to me in my future career.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h1><a name="_Toc352593104"><span lang=EN-US>5.2<span style='mso-tab-count:
1'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Future Work</span></a></h1>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The smartphone application that I have
developed has met its main primary goals but I have identified some areas in
which I could improve or enhance the implementation of the project as a whole.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc352593105"><span lang=EN-US>Profile Editing</span></a></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>I would like to implement a means for users
to edit their profile details.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>This would involve making changes to both
the mobile application and PHP database interaction project. Addition of this
feature would make the application more well rounded and professional.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc352593106"><span lang=EN-US>Data Analytics</span></a></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>Another feature I would like to implement
is the harnessing of all of the dormant user location data stored in the MySQL
database. If statistical data was generated about this information there could
be a lot of data discovered such as possible Ôdangerous areasÕ or areas in
which falls are more likely to occur.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc352593107"><span lang=EN-US>Password Retrieval/Change</span></a></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>A feature that I think would greatly benefit
the usability as well as the longevity of the mobile application would be a
means for the user to retrieve a forgotten password using their email and/or
username. I think this feature would add a lot of value to the application as
it would increase the user retention.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

mso-border-bottom-themecolor:accent1;padding:0cm 0cm 4.0pt 0cm'>
